\index{GW::MATH::GCollision@{GW::MATH::GCollision}!IntersectLineToTriangleD@{IntersectLineToTriangleD}}
\index{IntersectLineToTriangleD@{IntersectLineToTriangleD}!GW::MATH::GCollision@{GW::MATH::GCollision}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{IntersectLineToTriangleD()}{IntersectLineToTriangleD()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{GReturn}} GW\+::\+MATH\+::\+GCollision\+::\+Intersect\+Line\+To\+TriangleD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_l_i_n_e_d}{MATH\+::\+GLINED}}}]{\+\_\+line,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_t_r_i_a_n_g_l_e_d}{MATH\+::\+GTRIANGLED}}}]{\+\_\+triangle,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{GCollision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Contact\+Point,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}} $\ast$}]{\+\_\+out\+Barycentric,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Direction,  }\item[{double \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Interval }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Intersect line to triangle. 

Test a line to a clockwise triangle by computing if the line pierces the triangle. A collision will only be detected if the line is non-\/coplanar to the triangle and it pierces the from front face (the line\textquotesingle{}s start point lies in front of the triangle and the line\textquotesingle{}s end lies in back of the triangle). Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs. If the line contacts the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. If the line does not contact the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+NO\+\_\+\+COLLISION}}. If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+line} & The line. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+triangle} & The triangle. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Result} & The out result. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Contact\+Point} & The out contact point. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Barycentric} & If non-\/null, the out barycentric. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Direction} & The out direction. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Interval} & The out interval along the direction.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_ggaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617ad0749aaba8b833466dfcbb0428e4f89c}{GReturn\+::\+SUCCESS}}} & The calculation succeeded. \\
\hline

Intersect line to plane. 

Test a line to a plane by computing the interval along the line that intersects the plane. Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs. If the line contacts the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. If the line is coplanar to the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+NO\+\_\+\+COLLISION}}. If the line lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+BELOW}}. If the line lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+ABOVE}}.

Intersect line to sphere. 

Test a line to a sphere by computing the closest point on that line to the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center and reducing the query to a point to sphere check. Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs. If the line contacts the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. Intersect line to capsule.

Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs. Intersect line to AABB. 

Test a line to an AABB by checking if any section of the line lies within the AABB\textquotesingle{}s bounds. Provides the point of contact along with the normalized direction and interval along that direction the contact occurs. If the line contacts the AABB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. If the line does not contact the AABB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+NO\+\_\+\+COLLISION}}. If the function succeeds, the return value is SUCCESS. If the function fails, the return value is FAILURE. This would occur when the line degenerates to a point.

Intersect ray to triangle. 

Test a ray to a clockwise triangle by computing if the ray\textquotesingle{}s path intersects the triangle. Provides the point of contact along with the interval the contact occurs on the ray. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path contacts the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path does not contact the triangle, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+NO\+\_\+\+COLLISION}}. If the out barycentric argument is valid, the barycentric coordinates is stored in it.

Intersect ray to plane. 

Test a ray to a plane by computing if the ray\textquotesingle{}s path pierces the plane. Provides the point of contact along with the interval the contact occurs on the ray. If the ray contacts the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. If the ray is coplanar to the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+NO\+\_\+\+COLLISION}}. If the ray lies below the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5aa25949e21299b84cc33c4b00c740f08f}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+BELOW}}. If the ray lies above the plane, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5ac2d92b81beeac9bfc89fb870c1a20767}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+ABOVE}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{GReturn}} GW\+::\+MATH\+::\+GCollision\+::\+Intersect\+Ray\+To\+SphereD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_r_a_y_d}{MATH\+::\+GRAYD}}}]{\+\_\+ray,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_s_p_h_e_r_e_d}{MATH\+::\+GSPHERED}}}]{\+\_\+sphere,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{GCollision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Contact\+Point,  }\item[{double \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Interval }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Intersect ray to sphere. 

Tests if a collision exists between ray to sphere by using the quadratic formula to determine if there are any points of intersection (roots). Provides the point of contact along with the interval the contact occurs on the ray. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path contacts the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path does not contact the sphere, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+NO\+\_\+\+COLLISION}}.

Intersect ray to capsule. 

Test a ray to a capsule by computing the closest points on the ray\textquotesingle{}s path to the capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line and reduces the query to a point to sphere test. Provides the point of contact along with the interval the contact occurs on the ray. If the ray\textquotesingle{}s path contacts the capsule, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. {\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{GReturn}} GW\+::\+MATH\+::\+GCollision\+::\+Intersect\+Sphere\+To\+SphereD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_s_p_h_e_r_e_d}{MATH\+::\+GSPHERED}}}]{\+\_\+sphere1,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_s_p_h_e_r_e_d}{MATH\+::\+GSPHERED}}}]{\+\_\+sphere2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{GCollision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Contact\+Closest1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Contact\+Closest2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Direction,  }\item[{double \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Distance }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Intersect sphere to sphere. 

Test a sphere to sphere by checking the distance between their centers and the sum of their radii. Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface, the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. If the spheres contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. If the spheres do not contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+NO\+\_\+\+COLLISION}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+sphere1} & The first sphere. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+sphere2} & The second sphere. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Result} & The out result. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Contact\+Closest1} & The first out contact closest. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Contact\+Closest2} & The second out contact closest. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Direction} & The out direction. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Distance} & The out distance.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{GReturn}} GW\+::\+MATH\+::\+GCollision\+::\+Intersect\+Sphere\+To\+CapsuleD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_s_p_h_e_r_e_d}{MATH\+::\+GSPHERED}}}]{\+\_\+sphere,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_c_a_p_s_u_l_e_d}{MATH\+::\+GCAPSULED}}}]{\+\_\+capsule,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5}{GCollision\+Check}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Result,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Contact\+Closest1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Contact\+Closest2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Direction,  }\item[{double \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Distance }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Intersect sphere to capsule. 

Test a sphere to capsule by checking the distance between each\textquotesingle{}s center structures and the sum of their radii. Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface, the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. If the sphere contacts the capsule, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. If the sphere does not contact the capsule, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+NO\+\_\+\+COLLISION}}.

\hline

Intersect sphere to AABB. 

Test a sphere to an AABB by computing the distance from the AABB\textquotesingle{}s boundary to the sphere\textquotesingle{}s center and computing if that distance is within the sphere\textquotesingle{}s radius. Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface, the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. If the sphere contacts the AABB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. If the sphere does not contact the AABB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+NO\+\_\+\+COLLISION}}.

Intersect capsule to capsule. 

Test a capsule to another capsule by computing the closest points on each capsule\textquotesingle{}s center line and performing a sphere to sphere test. Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface, the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. If the capsules contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. Intersect capsule to AABB.

Intersect capsule to OBB.

Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface, the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. If the capsule contacts the OBB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. If the capsule does not contact the OBB, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+NO\+\_\+\+COLLISION}}.

Intersect AABB to AABB. 

Test an AABB to an AABB by checking if they overlap on all three axes. Provides the minimal translation information\+: two points on each shape\textquotesingle{}s surface,the direction the two points form, and distance required to translate the second shape to where the surfaces barely contact. If the AABBs contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5afc3ca10632f0c7aa3aaea07a234377db}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+COLLISION}}. If the AABBs don\textquotesingle{}t contact, the out result is \mbox{\hyperlink{class_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_collision_aaa1cd21a913c20e338cea128ae62eba5a874a40b8eb0a1602fae9e93767a85f08}{GCollision\+Check\+::\+NO\+\_\+\+COLLISION}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{BarycentricD()}{BarycentricD()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{group___g_return_values_gaf46a07bcad99edbe1e92a9fc99078617}{GReturn}} GW\+::\+MATH\+::\+GCollision\+::\+BarycentricD (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}}}]{\+\_\+a,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}}}]{\+\_\+b,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}}}]{\+\_\+c,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}}}]{\+\_\+p,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_w_1_1_m_a_t_h_1_1_g_v_e_c_t_o_r_d}{MATH\+::\+GVECTORD}} \&}]{\+\_\+out\+Barycentric }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Compute the barycentric coordinates of a point to triangle. 

Compute the barycentric coordinates given three points of a triangle with a point in respect to that triangle. Both triangle and point must be coplanar. The result is stored in a vector representing the barycentric coords. If the function succeeds, the return value is SUCCESS. If the function fails, the return value is FAILURE. This would occur when the triangle is degenerate.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+a} & The first point of a triangle. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+b} & The second point of a triangle. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+c} & The third point of a triangle. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em \+\_\+p} & The point coplanar with the triangle points. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \+\_\+out\+Barycentric} & The out barycentric coordinates.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
